     1	#!/usr/bin/env node
     2	// Assemble a ClaudeVille character sheet (8 dirs × 10 rows × 92px = 736×920)
     3	// from a pixellab MCP character ZIP.
     4	//
     5	// Pixellab ZIP layout (verified 2026-04-27):
     6	//   metadata.json
     7	//   rotations/<dir>.png                                          (S × S, S = source canvas)
     8	//   animations/animating-<uuid>/<dir>/frame_NNN.png              (S × S each)
     9	//
    10	// We map the two animations by FRAME COUNT:
    11	//   6 frames per direction → walk
    12	//   4 frames per direction → breathing-idle
    13	//
    14	// Usage:
    15	//   node scripts/sprites/generate-character-mcp.mjs --id=<sprite-id> --zip=<path-to-zip>
    16	//   (or omit --zip and the script looks for output/character-mcp-cache/<id>.zip)
    17	
    18	import { existsSync, mkdirSync, readFileSync, statSync, writeFileSync } from 'node:fs';
    19	import { dirname, join } from 'node:path';
    20	import { fileURLToPath } from 'node:url';
    21	import { spawnSync } from 'node:child_process';
    22	import { PNG } from 'pngjs';
    23	import yaml from 'js-yaml';
    24	
    25	const repoRoot = fileURLToPath(new URL('../..', import.meta.url));
    26	const cacheRoot = join(repoRoot, 'output', 'character-mcp-cache');
    27	const spritesRoot = join(repoRoot, 'claudeville', 'assets', 'sprites', 'characters');
    28	const manifestPath = join(repoRoot, 'claudeville', 'assets', 'sprites', 'manifest.yaml');
    29	
    30	const DIRECTIONS = ['south', 'south-east', 'east', 'north-east', 'north', 'north-west', 'west', 'south-west'];
    31	const CELL = 92;
    32	const WALK_FRAMES = 6;
    33	const IDLE_FRAMES = 4;
    34	const COLS = DIRECTIONS.length;
    35	const ROWS = WALK_FRAMES + IDLE_FRAMES;
    36	const args = new Set(process.argv.slice(2));
    37	const allowUnmanifested = args.has('--allow-unmanifested');
    38	const dryRun = args.has('--dry-run');
    39	
    40	function arg(name, fallback) {
    41	    const found = process.argv.find((a) => a.startsWith(`--${name}=`));
    42	    return found ? found.slice(name.length + 3) : fallback;
    43	}
    44	
    45	const id = arg('id', null);
    46	if (!id) { console.error('Missing --id=<sprite-id>'); process.exit(1); }
    47	const zipPath = arg('zip', join(cacheRoot, `${id}.zip`));
    48	
    49	main().catch((err) => { console.error(err.stack || err.message); process.exit(1); });
    50	
    51	async function main() {
    52	    assertManifested(id);
    53	    if (!existsSync(zipPath)) throw new Error(`ZIP not found: ${zipPath}`);
    54	    if (dryRun) {
    55	        console.log(`[character-mcp] dry run: ${id} is manifest-backed; ZIP exists at ${zipPath}`);
    56	        return;
    57	    }
    58	    let extractDir = zipPath;
    59	    if (!statSync(zipPath).isDirectory()) {
    60	        extractDir = join(cacheRoot, `${id}-extracted`);
    61	        mkdirSync(extractDir, { recursive: true });
    62	        const unzip = spawnSync('unzip', ['-o', '-q', zipPath, '-d', extractDir], { stdio: 'inherit' });
    63	        if (unzip.error) throw unzip.error;
    64	        if (unzip.status !== 0) throw new Error(`unzip failed with exit code ${unzip.status}`);
    65	    }
    66	
    67	    const meta = JSON.parse(readFileSync(join(extractDir, 'metadata.json'), 'utf8'));
    68	    const SOURCE = meta.character.size.width;
    69	    if (SOURCE < CELL) throw new Error(`Source canvas ${SOURCE} smaller than cell ${CELL}`);
    70	
    71	    // Merge all animations by frame count: a single template (walk/idle) may be
    72	    // split across multiple animation IDs if some directions failed and were
    73	    // re-queued separately. Build per-direction frame lists by union.
    74	    const walkByDir = {};
    75	    const idleByDir = {};
    76	    for (const [, dirs] of Object.entries(meta.frames.animations)) {
    77	        for (const [dir, frames] of Object.entries(dirs)) {
    78	            if (frames.length === WALK_FRAMES && !walkByDir[dir]) walkByDir[dir] = frames;
    79	            else if (frames.length === IDLE_FRAMES && !idleByDir[dir]) idleByDir[dir] = frames;
    80	        }
    81	    }
    82	
    83	    const sheet = new PNG({ width: CELL * COLS, height: CELL * ROWS });
    84	    sheet.data.fill(0);
    85	
    86	    for (let col = 0; col < COLS; col++) {
    87	        const dir = DIRECTIONS[col];
    88	
    89	        // Walk rows 0..5
    90	        const walkFrames = walkByDir[dir];
    91	        if (!walkFrames || walkFrames.length !== WALK_FRAMES) {
    92	            throw new Error(`walk animation missing direction ${dir} or wrong frame count`);
    93	        }
    94	        for (let f = 0; f < WALK_FRAMES; f++) {
    95	            const frame = readPng(join(extractDir, walkFrames[f]));
    96	            const cropped = cropCenter(frame, SOURCE);
    97	            blit(cropped, sheet, col * CELL, f * CELL);
    98	        }
    99	
   100	        // Idle rows 6..9
   101	        const idleFrames = idleByDir[dir];
   102	        if (!idleFrames || idleFrames.length !== IDLE_FRAMES) {
   103	            throw new Error(`idle animation missing direction ${dir} or wrong frame count`);
   104	        }
   105	        for (let f = 0; f < IDLE_FRAMES; f++) {
   106	            const frame = readPng(join(extractDir, idleFrames[f]));
   107	            const cropped = cropCenter(frame, SOURCE);
   108	            blit(cropped, sheet, col * CELL, (WALK_FRAMES + f) * CELL);
   109	        }
   110	    }
   111	
   112	    const outPath = join(spritesRoot, id, 'sheet.png');
   113	    mkdirSync(dirname(outPath), { recursive: true });
   114	    writeFileSync(outPath, PNG.sync.write(sheet));
   115	    console.log(`wrote ${outPath} (${CELL * COLS}×${CELL * ROWS}, source=${SOURCE})`);
   116	}
   117	
   118	function readPng(p) {
   119	    if (!existsSync(p)) throw new Error(`missing ${p}`);
   120	    return PNG.sync.read(readFileSync(p));
   121	}
   122	
   123	function assertManifested(spriteId) {
   124	    const manifest = yaml.load(readFileSync(manifestPath, 'utf8'));
   125	    const ids = new Set((manifest.characters || []).map((entry) => entry?.id).filter(Boolean));
   126	    if (ids.has(spriteId)) return;
   127	
   128	    const message = `unmanifested character ID: ${spriteId}`;
   129	    if (!allowUnmanifested) {
   130	        throw new Error(`${message}; pass --allow-unmanifested only for scratch assets`);
   131	    }
   132	    console.warn(`[character-mcp] WARNING: ${message}`);
   133	}
   134	
   135	// Center-crop a CELL×CELL window from a SOURCE×SOURCE frame.
   136	function cropCenter(src, source) {
   137	    if (src.width !== source || src.height !== source) {
   138	        throw new Error(`expected ${source}×${source}, got ${src.width}×${src.height}`);
   139	    }
   140	    const off = Math.floor((source - CELL) / 2);
   141	    const out = new PNG({ width: CELL, height: CELL });
   142	    out.data.fill(0);
   143	    for (let y = 0; y < CELL; y++) {
   144	        for (let x = 0; x < CELL; x++) {
   145	            const sxx = off + x;
   146	            const syy = off + y;
   147	            const si = (src.width * syy + sxx) << 2;
   148	            const di = (CELL * y + x) << 2;
   149	            out.data[di] = src.data[si];
   150	            out.data[di + 1] = src.data[si + 1];
   151	            out.data[di + 2] = src.data[si + 2];
   152	            out.data[di + 3] = src.data[si + 3];
   153	        }
   154	    }
   155	    return out;
   156	}
   157	
   158	function blit(src, dst, dx, dy) {
   159	    for (let y = 0; y < src.height; y++) {
   160	        for (let x = 0; x < src.width; x++) {
   161	            const si = (src.width * y + x) << 2;
   162	            if (src.data[si + 3] === 0) continue;
   163	            const dxx = dx + x;
   164	            const dyy = dy + y;
   165	            if (dxx < 0 || dyy < 0 || dxx >= dst.width || dyy >= dst.height) continue;
   166	            const di = (dst.width * dyy + dxx) << 2;
   167	            dst.data[di] = src.data[si];
   168	            dst.data[di + 1] = src.data[si + 1];
   169	            dst.data[di + 2] = src.data[si + 2];
   170	            dst.data[di + 3] = src.data[si + 3];
   171	        }
   172	    }
   173	}

   165	function drawCharacter(png, x0, y0, spec, direction, walking, frame) {
   166	    const front = ['s', 'se', 'sw'].includes(direction);
   167	    const back = ['n', 'ne', 'nw'].includes(direction);
   168	    const side = ['e', 'w'].includes(direction);
   169	    const sideSign = ['e', 'ne', 'se'].includes(direction) ? 1 : ['w', 'nw', 'sw'].includes(direction) ? -1 : 0;
   170	    const step = walking ? [0, 4, 7, 3, -4, -7][frame % 6] : 0;
   171	    const bob = walking ? (frame % 3 === 2 ? -1 : 0) : Math.round(Math.sin(frame * Math.PI / 2) * 1);
   172	    const cx = x0 + 46;
   173	    const feetY = y0 + 78 + bob;
   174	    const headY = y0 + 28 + bob;
   175	
   176	    ellipse(png, cx, feetY + 2, 17, 5, '#05080c', 82);
   177	    rect(png, cx - 5 + step, feetY - 13, 5, 14, spec.robeDark);
   178	    rect(png, cx + 1 - step, feetY - 13, 5, 14, spec.robeDark);
   179	    rect(png, cx - 7 + step, feetY - 2, 7, 3, '#151515');
   180	    rect(png, cx + 1 - step, feetY - 2, 7, 3, '#151515');
   181	
   182	    const capeShift = sideSign * 4;
   183	    polygon(png, [
   184	        [cx - 15 - capeShift, y0 + 39 + bob],
   185	        [cx + 15 - capeShift, y0 + 39 + bob],
   186	        [cx + 12 - capeShift, feetY - 6],
   187	        [cx - 12 - capeShift, feetY - 6],
   188	    ], spec.robeDark, 235);
   189	
   190	    if (spec.family === 'claude') drawClaudeBody(png, cx, y0, feetY, headY, spec, front, back, sideSign, step, bob);
   191	    else if (spec.family === 'gemini') drawGeminiBody(png, cx, y0, feetY, headY, spec, front, back, sideSign, step, bob);
   192	    else drawCodexBody(png, cx, y0, feetY, headY, spec, front, back, side, sideSign, step, bob);
   193	}
   194	
   195	function assertManifested(ids) {
   196	    const manifestIds = collectManifestIds();
   197	    const unmanifested = ids.filter((id) => !manifestIds.has(id));
   198	    if (!unmanifested.length) return;
   199	
   200	    const message = `unmanifested sprite IDs: ${unmanifested.join(', ')}`;
   201	    if (!allowUnmanifested) {
   202	        throw new Error(`${message}; pass --allow-unmanifested only for scratch assets`);
   203	    }
   204	    console.warn(`[baseline] WARNING: ${message}`);
   205	}
   206	
   207	function collectManifestIds() {
   208	    const manifest = yaml.load(readFileSync(manifestPath, 'utf8'));
   209	    const ids = new Set();
   210	    for (const key of ['characters', 'accessories', 'statusOverlays', 'buildings', 'props', 'vegetation', 'terrain', 'bridges', 'atmosphere']) {
   211	        for (const entry of manifest[key] || []) {
   212	            if (entry?.id) ids.add(entry.id);
   213	        }
   214	    }
   215	    return ids;
   216	}
   217	
   218	function drawClaudeBody(png, cx, y0, feetY, headY, spec, front, back, sideSign, step, bob) {
   219	    polygon(png, [[cx - 13, y0 + 41 + bob], [cx + 13, y0 + 41 + bob], [cx + 10, feetY - 8], [cx - 10, feetY - 8]], spec.robe);
   220	    rect(png, cx - 8, y0 + 45 + bob, 16, 3, spec.trim);
   221	    line(png, cx, y0 + 43 + bob, cx, feetY - 12, spec.trim, 2);
   222

   319	function writePng(path, png) {
   320	    mkdirSync(dirname(path), { recursive: true });
   321	    writeFileSync(path, PNG.sync.write(png));
   322	    console.log(`wrote ${path.replace(repoRoot + '/', '')}`);
   323	}
   324	
   325	function color(hex, alpha = 255) {
   326	    const h = hex.replace('#', '');
   327	    return [parseInt(h.slice(0, 2), 16), parseInt(h.slice(2, 4), 16), parseInt(h.slice(4, 6), 16), alpha];
   328	}
   329	
   330	function px(png, x, y, hex, alpha = 255) {
   331	    x = Math.round(x); y = Math.round(y);
   332	    if (x < 0 || y < 0 || x >= png.width || y >= png.height) return;
   333	    const [r, g, b, a] = color(hex, alpha);
   334	    const idx = (png.width * y + x) << 2;
   335	    const inv = 255 - a;
   336	    png.data[idx] = Math.round((r * a + png.data[idx] * inv) / 255);
   337	    png.data[idx + 1] = Math.round((g * a + png.data[idx + 1] * inv) / 255);
   338	    png.data[idx + 2] = Math.round((b * a + png.data[idx + 2] * inv) / 255);
   339	    png.data[idx + 3] = Math.min(255, a + Math.round(png.data[idx + 3] * inv / 255));
   340	}
   341	
   342	function rect(png, x, y, w, h, hex, alpha = 255) {
   343	    for (let yy = Math.round(y); yy < Math.round(y + h); yy++)
   344	        for (let xx = Math.round(x); xx < Math.round(x + w); xx++)
   345	            px(png, xx, yy, hex, alpha);
   346	}
   347	
   348	function ellipse(png, cx, cy, rx, ry, hex, alpha = 255) {
   349	    for (let y = Math.floor(cy - ry); y <= Math.ceil(cy + ry); y++)
   350	        for (let x = Math.floor(cx - rx); x <= Math.ceil(cx + rx); x++)
   351	            if (((x - cx) ** 2) / (rx ** 2) + ((y - cy) ** 2) / (ry ** 2) <= 1)
   352	                px(png, x, y, hex, alpha);
   353	}
   354	
   355	function line(png, x0, y0, x1, y1, hex, width = 1, alpha = 255) {
   356	    x0 = Math.round(x0); y0 = Math.round(y0); x1 = Math.round(x1); y1 = Math.round(y1);
   357	    const dx = Math.abs(x1 - x0), sx = x0 < x1 ? 1 : -1;
   358	    const dy = -Math.abs(y1 - y0), sy = y0 < y1 ? 1 : -1;
   359	    let err = dx + dy;
   360	    while (true) {
   361	        rect(png, x0 - Math.floor(width / 2), y0 - Math.floor(width / 2), width, width, hex, alpha);
   362	        if (x0 === x1 && y0 === y1) break;
   363	        const e2 = 2 * err;
   364	        if (e2 >= dy) { err += dy; x0 += sx; }
   365	        if (e2 <= dx) { err += dx; y0 += sy; }
   366	    }
   367	}
   368	
   369	function polygon(png, points, hex, alpha = 255) {
   370	    const minY = Math.floor(Math.min(...points.map(p => p[1])));
   371	    const maxY = Math.ceil(Math.max(...points.map(p => p[1])));
   372	    for (let y = minY; y <= maxY; y++) {
   373	        const xs = [];
   374	        for (let i = 0; i < points.length; i++) {
   375	            const [x1, y1] = points[i];
   376	            const [x2, y2] = points[(i + 1) % points.length];
   377	            if ((y1 <= y && y2 > y) || (y2 <= y && y1 > y)) {
   378	                xs.push(x1 + (y - y1) * (x2 - x1) / (y2 - y1));
   379	            }
   380	        }
   381	        xs.sort((a, b) => a - b);
   382	        for (let i = 0; i < xs.length; i += 2) {
   383	            for (let x = Math.ceil(xs[i]); x <= Math.floor(xs[i + 1]); x++) px(png, x, y, hex, alpha);
   384	        }
   385	    }
   386	}
   387	
   388	function diamond(png, cx, cy, r, hex, alpha = 255) {
   389	    polygon(png, [[cx, cy - r], [cx + r, cy], [cx, cy + r], [cx - r, cy]], hex, alpha);
   390	}
   391	
   392	function star(png, cx, cy, r, hex, alpha = 255) {
   393	    line(png, cx - r, cy, cx + r, cy, hex, 1, alpha);
   394	    line(png, cx, cy - r, cx, cy + r, hex, 1, alpha);
   395	    px(png, cx - 1, cy - 1, hex, alpha);
   396	    px(png, cx + 1, cy + 1, hex, alpha);
   397	}
   398	
   399	function gear(png, cx, cy, r, hex) {
   400	    ellipse(png, cx, cy, r, r, hex, 230);
   401	    for (let i = 0; i < 8; i++) {
   402	        const a = i * Math.PI / 4;
   403	        rect(png, cx + Math.cos(a) * r - 1, cy + Math.sin(a) * r - 1, 3, 3, hex, 240);
   404	    }
   405	    ellipse(png, cx, cy, Math.max(2, r - 4), Math.max(2, r - 4), '#12353b', 255);
   406	}

   125	function assertManifested(ids) {
   126	    const manifestIds = collectManifestIds();
   127	    const unmanifested = ids.filter((id) => !manifestIds.has(id));
   128	    if (!unmanifested.length) return;
   129	
   130	    const message = `unmanifested sprite IDs: ${unmanifested.join(', ')}`;
   131	    if (!allowUnmanifested) {
   132	        throw new Error(`${message}; pass --allow-unmanifested only for scratch assets`);
   133	    }
   134	    console.warn(`[pixellab-revamp] WARNING: ${message}`);
   135	}
   136	
   137	function collectManifestIds() {
   138	    const manifest = yaml.load(readFileSync(manifestPath, 'utf8'));
   139	    const ids = new Set();
   140	    for (const key of ['characters', 'accessories', 'statusOverlays', 'buildings', 'props', 'vegetation', 'terrain', 'bridges', 'atmosphere']) {
   141	        for (const entry of manifest[key] || []) {
   142	            if (entry?.id) ids.add(entry.id);
   143	        }
   144	    }
   145	    return ids;
   146	}

   148	function readToken() {
   149	    const envPath = join(repoRoot, '.dev.vars');
   150	    if (!existsSync(envPath)) throw new Error('.dev.vars not found');
   151	    const env = Object.fromEntries(
   152	        readFileSync(envPath, 'utf8')
   153	            .split(/\r?\n/)
   154	            .map((line) => line.trim())
   155	            .filter((line) => line && !line.startsWith('#') && line.includes('='))
   156	            .map((line) => {
   157	                const idx = line.indexOf('=');
   158	                return [line.slice(0, idx), line.slice(idx + 1).replace(/^["']|["']$/g, '')];
   159	            })
   160	    );
   161	    const token = env.PIXELLAB_API_TOKEN || env.PIXELLAB_AUTHORIZATION?.replace(/^Bearer\s+/i, '');
   162	    if (!token) throw new Error('PIXELLAB_API_TOKEN or PIXELLAB_AUTHORIZATION missing in .dev.vars');
   163	    return token;
   164	}
   165	
   166	async function generateMapConcept(token) {
   167	    const out = join(cacheRoot, 'town-concept.png');
   168	    if (!force && existsSync(out)) {
   169	        console.log(`[pixellab-revamp] cached map concept ${relativeOut(out)}`);
   170	        return;
   171	    }
   172	    if (skipApi) return;
   173	    const png = await pixflux(token, {
   174	        cacheKey: 'town-concept.raw.png',
   175	        description: [
   176	            'top-down old-school fantasy RPG village concept map for ClaudeVille',
   177	            'central stone civic plaza with command keep, city hall, and task board',
   178	            'river crossing through town, harbor lighthouse and docks on the east water edge',
   179	            'forge row, token mine yard, scholars archive, observatory, sanctuary grove, arcane portal',
   180	            'clear readable district organization, winding roads, no labels, no text',
   181	        ].join(', '),
   182	        width: 400,
   183	        height: 400,
   184	        transparent: false,
   185	        seed: 82011,
   186	    });
   187	    writePng(out, png);
   188	}
   189	
   190	async function generateBuilding(token, spec) {
   191	    const cacheKey = `buildings/${spec.id}.raw.png`;
   192	    if (skipApi && !existsSync(join(cacheRoot, cacheKey))) return;
   193	    const raw = await pixflux(token, {
   194	        cacheKey,
   195	        description: `${STYLE}, ${spec.description}`,
   196	        width: spec.width,
   197	        height: spec.height,
   198	        transparent: true,
   199	        seed: hashSeed(spec.id),
   200	    });
   201	    const png = keyOutEdgeBackground(raw);
   202	
   203	    if (spec.kind === 'hero') {
   204	        const normalized = resizeNearest(png, spec.width, spec.height);
   205	        const cols = spec.cols || 3;
   206	        const rows = spec.rows || 2;
   207	        const cellW = Math.round(spec.width / cols);
   208	        const cellH = Math.round(spec.height / rows);
   209	        for (let r = 0; r < rows; r++) {
   210	            for (let c = 0; c < cols; c++) {
   211	                const tile = crop(normalized, c * cellW, r * cellH, cellW, cellH);
   212	                writePng(join(spritesRoot, 'buildings', spec.id, `base-${c}-${r}.png`), tile);
   213	            }
   214	        }
   215	    } else {
   216	        writePng(join(spritesRoot, 'buildings', spec.id, 'base.png'), resizeNearest(png, spec.width, spec.height));
   217	    }
   218	}
   219	
   220	async function generateCharacter(token, spec) {
   221	    const sheet = await pixflux(token, {
   222	        cacheKey: `characters/${spec.id}.sheet.raw.png`,
   223	        description: [
   224	            STYLE,
   225	            'complete transparent character animation sprite sheet',
   226	            `${spec.description}`,
   227	            `exact ${DIRECTIONS.length} columns for directions ${DIRECTIONS.join(', ')}`,
   228	            `${WALK_ROWS + IDLE_ROWS} rows total`,
   229	            `first ${WALK_ROWS} rows are a walk cycle with alternating legs, arms, robe hem, and planted foot contact`,
   230	            `last ${IDLE_ROWS} rows are breathing idle poses`,
   231	            `${CELL}px square cells, no grid lines, no labels, no text`,
   232	        ].join(', '),
   233	        width: CELL * DIRECTIONS.length,
   234	        height: CELL * (WALK_ROWS + IDLE_ROWS),
   235	        transparent: true,
   236	        seed: hashSeed(spec.id),
   237	    });
   238	    writePng(
   239	        join(spritesRoot, 'characters', spec.id, 'sheet.png'),
   240	        resizeNearest(sheet, CELL * DIRECTIONS.length, CELL * (WALK_ROWS + IDLE_ROWS))
   241	    );
   242	}
   243	
   244	function keyOutEdgeBackground(src) {
   245	    const out = clonePng(src);
   246	    const edgeSeedColors = sampleEdgeBackgroundColors(out);
   247	    if (edgeSeedColors.length === 0) return out;
   248	
   249	    const visited = new Uint8Array(out.width * out.height);


</details>

## POST /create-character-with-8-directions
**Create character with 8 directions**
Tags: Character from template

Generate a character or object facing 8 directions (all cardinal and diagonal directions).

### Parameters

### Request Body
- `description`: string (minLen=1, maxLen=2000) (required)
  Description of the character or object to generate
- `image_size`: object (required)
- `image_size.width`: integer (min=16.0, max=128.0) (required)
  Character size in pixels. Canvas will be ~40% larger to make room for animations.
- `image_size.height`: integer (min=16.0, max=128.0) (required)
  Character size in pixels. Canvas will be ~40% larger to make room for animations.
- `mode`: string | null (optional)
  Generation mode. "standard" uses template-based skeleton generation (1 generation). "pro" uses AI reference-based generation for higher quality (costs 20-40 generations depending on size). Pro mode ignores outline, shading, detail, proportions, and text_guidance_scale.
- `async_mode`: boolean | null (optional)
  Process asynchronously (always true - no synchronous processing yet)
- `text_guidance_scale`: number | null (optional)


</details>

## POST /animate-character
**Animate character**
Tags: Character from template

Animate an existing character with multiple frames showing movement or action.

### Parameters

### Request Body
- `character_id`: string (required)
  ID of existing character to animate
- `animation_name`: string | null (optional)
  Name for this animation (defaults to action_description if not provided)
- `description`: string | null (optional)
  Description of the character or object to animate (uses character's original if not specified)
- `action_description`: string | null (optional)
  Action description (e.g., 'walking', 'running', 'jumping'). Required for custom mode (when template_animation_id is omitted). For template mode, defaults to a description based on the template.
- `async_mode`: boolean | null (optional)
  Process in background (always true - no foreground processing yet)
- `mode`: string | null (optional)
  Animation mode. "template": skeleton-based from template_animation_id (1 gen/direction). "v3": custom animation from action_description with frame_count control. "pro": custom animation that generates directions sequentially, using completed sides as reference (20-40 gen/direction). Auto-detected: template if template_animation_id is provided, v3 otherwise.
- `template_animation_id`: string | null (optional)
  Animation template ID. Required for template mode. Available: `angry`, `attack`, `attack-back`, `attack-left`, `attack-right`, `backflip`, `bark`, `breathing-idle`, `cross-punch`, `crouched-walking`, ...
- `frame_count`: integer | null (optional)
  Number of animation frames (4-16, must be even). Only used in v3 mode.
- `text_guidance_scale`: number | null (optional)
  How closely to follow the text description (higher = more faithful). Template mode only.
- `outline`: string | null (optional)
  Outline style (uses character's original if not specified). Template mode only.
- `shading`: string | null (optional)
  Shading style (uses character's original if not specified). Template mode only.


</details>

4. `POST /animate-character` with `template_animation_id="breathing-idle"`
5. Poll `GET /characters/{id}` until both animations show progress: 100
6. Download ZIP from `GET /characters/{id}/zip`
7. Run `generate-character-mcp.mjs --id=agent.kimi.base --zip=<path>`

      headers: { Authorization: `Bearer ${TOKEN}` }

const TOKEN = process.env.TOKEN;
const CHAR_ID = '7d28f38b-d700-4e8d-8f9e-3e043a14e6a3';
const API = 'https://api.pixellab.ai/v2';

async function poll() {
  for (let i = 0; i < 60; i++) {
    const res = await fetch(`${API}/characters/${CHAR_ID}`, {
      headers: { Authorization: `Bearer ${TOKEN}` }
    });
    const data = await res.json();

    console.log(`Poll ${i + 1}: ${anims.length} animations. ${progress}`);
    if (anims.length >= 2 && anims.every(a => a.progress === 100)) {
      console.log('All animations complete!');
      console.log('ZIP URL:', data.zip_url || `${API}/characters/${CHAR_ID}/zip`);
      return data;
    }
    await new Promise(r => setTimeout(r, 60000));
  }
  throw new Error('Polling timed out after 60 minutes');
}

const CHAR_ID = '7d28f38b-d700-4e8d-8f9e-3e043a14e6a3';
const API = 'https://api.pixellab.ai/v2';

async function poll() {
  for (let i = 0; i < 60; i++) {
    const res = await fetch(`${API}/characters/${CHAR_ID}`, {
      headers: { Authorization: `Bearer ${TOKEN}` }
    });
    const data = await res.json();
    const anims = data.animations || [];
    const progress = anims.map(a => `${a.animation_name || a.id}: ${a.progress}%`).join(', ');
    console.log(`Poll ${i + 1}: ${anims.length} animations. ${progress}`);
    if (anims.length >= 2 && anims.every(a => a.progress === 100)) {
      console.log('All animations complete!');
      console.log('ZIP URL:', data.zip_url || `${API}/characters/${CHAR_ID}/zip`);
      return data;
    }
    await new Promise(r => setTimeout(r, 60000));
  }
  throw new Error('Polling timed out after 60 minutes');
}

poll().catch(e => { console.error(e); process.exit(1); });
EOF
